visibleTop\n}\n\n\t\n</script>\n\n<script type=\"text/javascript\" charset=\"UTF-8\" src=\"http://maps.google.com/maps-api-v3/api/js/28/10/common.js\"></script><script type=\"text/javascript\" Presenters at Finovate events run the gamut of financial technology. What is the refund policy for attendee tickets? </p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"col-md-6 col-md-offset-1\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>A. Assuming that there is no one at your company that youâd like to transfer your ticket to, the refund policy for FinovateSpring is as follows:</p>\n<ul>\n<ul>\n<li>For cancellations requested on or prior to March 3, 2017, we will refund 100% of the fee.</li>\n<li>For cancellations between March 4, 2017 and March 31, 2017, we will refund 50% of the fee.</li>\n<li>For cancellations on or after April 1, 2017, we will not be able to refund any of the fee, but we will still be able to transfer your ticket to another member of your team.</li>\n<li>If youâd like to request a refund, please complete the form <a href=\"https://spring2017.finovate.com/ticketrefundform/\">here</a>.</li>\n</ul>\n</ul>\n<p>Please note: We will always honor cancellation requests made within 48 hours of purchase.</p>\n \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"row\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"col-md-6 col-md-offset-1\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"question\">Q. Is there an official hotel for FinovateSpring, or have you negotiated a special rate at a nearby hotel?  </p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"col-md-6 col-md-offset-1\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>A. There is no official hotel for FinovateSpring, and we have not negotiated any special rates at local hotels. In the past, weâve found that online travel websites are consistently able to undercut our âspecialâ rates, so we recommend using Expedia, Hotwire, Priceline, Travelocity, etc. to find a hotel that looks good to you. There are numerous hotels in the immediate vicinity of the venue at a variety of price points.</p>\n \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"row\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"col-md-6 col-md-offset-1\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"question\">Q: What is the application and selection process for Finovate events? </p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"col-md-6 col-md-offset-1\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>A: Good question! Finovate events are open to startups, established companies, and financial institutions with new fintech innovations, so the bar to get on stage is very high. Each company interested in demoing their new fintech at one of our events must submit a written application. We may also set up a quick screening phone call to make sure that we have a good understanding of the application and how the demo might look.</p>\n<p>When selecting companies, we look at several criteria: novelty (newness of the fintech), innovativeness (originality of the approach), potential (degree of impact in the fintech industry), wow/X/cool factor, and diversity (comparison to the number of companies in the same âspaceâ competing for a spot).</p>\n<p>For each event, we receive far more applications than we have demo spots to fill. Given this competiveness, one of the major keys to getting a spot is to have something new, innovative, and substantial to debut live on stage.</p>\n<p>If youâre interested in demoing at one of our events, please send an email to the appropriate email address: <a href=\"mailto:europe@finovate.com\">europe@finovate.com</a>, <a href=\"mailto:spring@finovate.com\">spring@finovate.com</a>, <a href=\"mailto:fall@finovate.com\">fall@finovate.com</a>, or <a href=\"mailto:asia@finovate.com\">asia@finovate.com</a>.</p>\n \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"row\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"col-md-6 col-md-offset-1\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"question\">Q: Can you tell me more about the city of San Jose? </p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"col-md-6 col-md-offset-1\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"p1\"><span class=\"s1\">A: Of course! Located in the heart of Silicon Valley, San Jose booms with innovation and boasts 300 days of sunshine per year. It is also home to many museums and entertainment venues, not to mention some good food. For more information, please visit <a href=\"http://sanjose.org/\" target=\"_blank\"><span class=\"s2\">sanjose.org</span></a> where youâll find city specifics (e.g. transportation options, calendar of events, current weather, etc.).</span></p>\n \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div> <!-- end .container div -->
